| 0:06:06| This is a resolution memorializing Officer David Seedler.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=366)|
| 0:06:11| Whereas Officer David Seedler passed away on December 31, 2012, at the age of 50,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=371)|
| 0:06:17| and whereas over the course of his 22 years of service in the Knox County Sheriff's Office,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=377)|
| 0:06:22| Officer David Seedler demonstrated the utmost professionalism, ability, and integrity while serving in several divisions| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=382)|
| 0:06:29| of the Sheriff's Office, including the jail, patrol, property, seizures, narcotics,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=389)|
| 0:06:34| and the past seven years in court services.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=394)|
| 0:06:37| And whereas Officer Seedler was an exemplary officer serving the citizens of Knox County with the passion| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=397)|
| 0:06:44| and dedication that went above and beyond the call of duty.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=404)|
| 0:06:48| And whereas Officer David Seedler felt it an honor every day to wear the uniform of the Knox County Sheriff's Office| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=408)|
| 0:06:56| and to serve alongside his fellow officers.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=416)|
| 0:06:59| And whereas Officer Seedler's honorable service and loyalty to Knox County| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=419)|
| 0:07:04| and the Knox County Sheriff's Office earned him the respect of all who had the pleasure of serving and working with him.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=424)|
| 0:07:10| Now, therefore, be it resolved by the Commission of Knox County as follows.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=430)|
| 0:07:14| The Commission of Knox County, on behalf of the people of Knox County,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=434)|
| 0:07:18| hereby memorializes Officer David Seedler for his many years in dedicated service to Knox County| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=438)|
| 0:07:25| and the Knox County Sheriff's Office and further conveys to his family, friends, and fellow officers| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=445)|

| 2:21:20| It's a total budget of just under $420 million.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8480)|
| 2:21:25| And so, therefore, it's an increase of about $13.3 million or just over 3%.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8485)|
| 2:21:30| As we began to develop this budget, we had lots of conversations.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8490)|
| 2:21:35| We had several budget meetings and forums out in the community| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8495)|
| 2:21:38| and heard back from people about their interests and priorities in this budget.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8498)|
| 2:21:42| I actually got a chance to talk to, I think,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8502)|
| 2:21:44| most of the commissioners over the last several months as we were looking at this budget and putting it together.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8504)|
| 2:21:49| And, essentially, there were four priorities that were identified for this budget.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8509)|
| 2:21:53| The first was enhancing educator compensation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8513)|
| 2:21:56| And more than half of that $13 million increase is budgeted toward that end.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8516)|
| 2:22:05| We recognize that we want to make sure that we provide our fine educators with compensation| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8525)|
| 2:22:14| that is commensurate with the value they provide and that is professional.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8534)|
| 2:22:18| Knox County Schools, as of this year, ranks 35th in the state of Tennessee in terms of our average teacher salary,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8538)|
| 2:22:25| and that's certainly not where we want to be.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8545)|
| 2:22:27| So this budget, we built into this budget two major components in terms of educator compensation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8547)|
| 2:22:35| First of all, there is a step increase for both certified and non-certified personnel in this budget.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8555)|
| 2:22:43| But then, in addition to that, there's a salary increase, a base salary increase,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8563)|
| 2:22:47| for our teachers of 1.5% at the beginning of the year and an additional 1% at mid-year.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8567)|
| 2:22:53| We believe that that will allow us to make progress in bringing our salaries to be more competitive| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8573)|
| 2:23:01| with some of the other school districts, even in our region, that pay, in some cases, considerably more.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8581)|
| 2:23:08| So we want to make some progress on the base salary, and we believe this budget will help us to do that.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8588)|
| 2:23:12| And then secondly, we want to continue our strategic compensation initiative| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8592)|
| 2:23:18| or our performance-based pay initiative that we've instituted.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8598)|
| 2:23:22| It's called APEX.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8602)|
| 2:23:23| It stands for Advanced Perform Excel, and it really is a way to incent and reward great teaching| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8603)|
| 2:23:31| and great outcomes for kids, and the dollars are budgeted and allocated in that way.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8611)|
| 2:23:37| So both of those things we're able to do within this budget that the board has adopted around educator compensation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8617)|
| 2:23:44| The second priority is sustaining instructional improvement initiatives,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWS130520?start=8624)|
